If you feel you are not at the right height after app launch, simply stand up, look forward, and say or tap \"Reset Floor Level\". \r\n\r\nYou could draw and talk to others and guess each others' drawings. Each full tank contains 100 paintballs. Try to move around to dodge incoming paintballs, or teleport to reposition.
